SQL> SELECT UC.CONSTRAINT_NAME, UC.TABLE_NAME, UCC.COLUMN_NAME,
  2  UC.CONSTRAINT_TYPE, UC.R_CONSTRAINT_NAME, UC.SEARCH_CONDITION
  3  FROM USER_CONSTRAINTS UC JOIN USER_CONS_COLUMNS UCC
  4  ON UC.CONSTRAINT_NAME = UCC.CONSTRAINT_NAME
  5  WHERE UC.TABLE_NAME = 'COUNTRIES'
  6  ;

  2  from employees e join (select department_id, max(salary) as salary

  2  (IN_EMPNO EMP.EMPNO%TYPE)
  3  RETURN EMP.SAL%TYPE
  4  IS
  5             OUT_SAL EMP.SAL%TYPE :=0;

  8             INTO OUT_SAL
  9             FROM EMP

  1  CREATE OR REPLACE PACKAGE BODY CURSOR_PKG
  2  AS
  3  PROCEDURE SP_JOB_HISTORY
  4  (
  5     IN_EMPLOYEE_ID IN EMPLOYEES.EMPOLYEE_ID%TYPE,
  6     OUT_CURSOR      IN OUT T_CURSOR
  7  )
  8  IS
  9  BEGIN
 10     OPEN OUT_CURSOR FOR
 11     SELECT E.FRIST_NAME ||' '|| E.LAST_NAME AS NAME
 12     ,JO.JOB_TITLE AS TITLE
 13     ,JH.START_DATE AS SDATE
 14     ,JH.END_DATE AS EDATE
 15     FROM EMPLOYEES E EJOIN JOB_HISTORY JH
 16             ON E.EMPLOYEE_DI = JH.EMLOYEE_ID
 17             JOIN JOBS JO
 18             ON JH.JOB_ID = JO.JOB_ID
 19     WHERE E.EMPLOYEE_ID = IN_EMPLOYEE_ID;
 20  END SP_JOB_HISTORY;
 21* END CURSOR_PKG;
 22  /

SQL> DECLARE
  2  V_NO NUMBER(4);
  3  V_NAME VARCHAR2(20);
  4  BEGIN
  5  SELECT EMPNO, ENAME
  6  INTO V_NO, V_NAME
  7  FROM EMP
